pub.</span><cite class="q0gngn-2 hbMmDq"><span class="q0gngn-3 bvPrfo"> </span></cite></figcaption></figure><p>Cold beer. Meat raffles. Ancient verandahs. Good dogs. How great are country pubs? Especially those which boost a community through top-notch food sourced locally (rather than deep-fried imported squid, say), cater to multiple generations and accommodate tourists. Like their city cousins, regional pubs are also changing. While there are still plenty of beaut yellow-tiled public bars with a choice of two to three taps, young gun hoteliers are increasingly selling just as much craft beer and cocktails as Tooheys, and weâre all for the shift. (Word around Jugiong way is that the Sir George has even introduced linen napkins.) Here are 10 of NSWâs best old and new-breed boozers.</p><h2><strong>Billinudgel Hotel</strong> </h2><p>They donât make them like the Nudge anymore. The self-described âlast of the good olâ country pubsâ is 20 minutes north of Byron Bay, but could be 100 years in the past. A place of faded photos, creaking floorboards, Chesterfield lounges and old logs fashioned into furniture. The beer garden can lift off with Anzac Day-level energy on the weekend. </p><p><strong>Best for: </strong>Tall tales and cold ones on the back deck. </p></div><div class="sc-147tfzb-0 frFHgZ bought the pub formerly known as the Coast Hotel. Lismore, The Eltham stands proud, and sometimes loud, in a tiny village. Live country rock is a regular feature in the beer garden, while inside is all wildflowers, weatherboard and vintage paraphernalia. Chef-in-residence Alanna Sapwell-Stone serves elevated pub dishes such as white pudding with duck egg and lentils, and five styled short-stay rooms complete the package.</p><p><strong>Best for:</strong> Modern country cooking and old-time Australian rockânâroll. </p><p><em>441 Eltham Road, Eltham, <a class="inline-link" href=https://www.elthampub.com.au/ rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">elthampub.com.au</a></em></p></div><div class="sc-147tfzb-0 frFHgZ adWrapper noPrint sc-1poyj9i-3 lfRhLg" data-testid="ad"><div class="sc-147tfzb-1 grIoTl"></div><small class="sc-147tfzb-2 fa-Dhrx">Advertisement</small></div><div class="sc-1hfqzg1-0 bpqJpD"><h2><strong>The Globe Hotel </strong></h2><p>A good pub should serve the community first, and The Globe looks after its locals with aplomb. bvPrfo">Supplied</span></cite></figcaption></figure><h2><strong>The Sir George </strong></h2></div><div class="sc-147tfzb-0 frFHgZ adWrapper noPrint sc-1poyj9i-3 lfRhLg" data-testid="ad"><div class="sc-147tfzb-1 grIoTl"></div><small class="sc-147tfzb-2 fa-Dhrx">Advertisement</small></div><div class="sc-1hfqzg1-0 bpqJpD"><p>There are few better ways to break up a road trip from Sydney to Just one minute off the Hume Highway, the 1850s-built tavern is open to all travellers happy to part with $435 to stay in one of the smartly renovated boutique barn rooms, or just drop in for a fireside pork cotoletta and Canberra District pinot. </p><p><strong>Best for:</strong> A road trip burger made on bread from the on-site artisan bakery. </p><p><em>320 Riverside Drive, Jugiong, <a class="inline-link" href=http://sirgeorge.com.au rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">sirgeorge.com.au</a></em></p><h2><strong>Southern Railway Hotel </strong></h2><p>This ancient local may well be home to the best Sunday pub roast in the state. Recent specials on the weekend menu have included stuffed lamb saddle, beef cheek hotpot and roast pheasant with duck-fat spuds. The new British chef, Paul Carr, is leading this roast revolution, and his âproperâ fish and chips are worth a detour too. </p></div><div class="sc-147tfzb-0 frFHgZ adWrapper noPrint sc-1poyj9i-3 lfRhLg" data-testid="ad"><div class="sc-147tfzb-1 grIoTl"></div><small class="sc-147tfzb-2 fa-Dhrx">Advertisement</small></div><div class="sc-1hfqzg1-0 bpqJpD"><p><strong>Best for:</strong> âButcherâs blockâ specials and<em> the</em> Sunday roast.</p><p><em>188 Sloane Street, Goulburn, <a class="inline-link" href=http://thesouthernrailwayhotel.com.au rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">thesouthernrailwayhotel.com.au</a></em></p><p><strong>With David Matthews and Lenny Ann Low</strong></p><aside data-testid="related-story" class="sc-18bmp0g-0 dyMfne"><div
